<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:1pt">

</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2020 Third Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Quarterly Performance Significantly Impacted by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> Pandemic </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Company Accelerates Progress on Strategic Priorities </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Estimated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact on the third quarter </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Adverse sales impact of approximately $700&nbsp;million to $750&nbsp;million, almost entirely from the
company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-U.S.</FONT> businesses </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Gross margin adversely impacted by shift from higher to lower margin categories, supply chain costs
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">SG&amp;A increased due to higher employee costs and social distancing and cleaning expenses
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Both operating income and adjusted operating income included an adverse impact of $700&nbsp;million to
$750&nbsp;million from the above items, or $0.61 to $0.65 per share, excluding impairment charges </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Most significant <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact was in UK market, requiring a review
resulting in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges of $2&nbsp;billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company accelerated investments in strategic priorities, preparing for future growth </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

in excess of $2.0&nbsp;billion by fiscal 2022, from previous target in excess of $1.8&nbsp;billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Additional highlights </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

the same period a year ago; Free cash flow increased 23.7&nbsp;percent to $2.4&nbsp;billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company introduced fiscal 2020 adjusted EPS guidance of $4.65 to $4.75 including estimated <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impacts of $1.03 to $1.14 per share </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><I></I></B>Company increased quarterly dividend by 2.2&nbsp;percent, to an annual rate of $1.87 per share and
suspended activity under its share repurchase program </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill., July&nbsp;9, 2020 - Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA)
today announced financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2020, which ended May&nbsp;31, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Executive Vice Chairman and CEO Stefano Pessina
said, &#147;Prior to the pandemic our financial performance for fiscal 2020 was on track with our expectations. However, this unprecedented global crisis led to a loss in the quarter as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">stay-at-home</FONT></FONT> orders affected all of our markets. I&#146;m very proud of how all of our teams mobilized and adapted to </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
deliver essential services in our communities across the world. Shopping patterns are evolving more rapidly than ever as consumers further embrace digital options, spurring us to accelerate our
ongoing investments in digital transformation and neighborhood health destinations. This includes our two recent announcements: a significant expansion of our primary care clinics collaboration with VillageMD, and our strategic partnership with
Microsoft and Adobe to launch a personalized omnichannel healthcare and shopping experience.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Estimated
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> Impact on WBA </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The adverse impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> on sales in the
quarter was approximately $700&nbsp;million to $750&nbsp;million, with the majority of the impact related to the Retail Pharmacy International division. This reflected a dramatic reduction in footfall in Boots UK stores - down 85&nbsp;percent in
April - as consumers were advised to leave home only for food and medicine. While most Boots stores remained open throughout the UK lockdown to provide communities with pharmacy and essential healthcare, our largest premium beauty and fragrance
counters were effectively closed. More than 100 stores, mainly in high street, station and airport locations, were temporarily closed as were nearly all of the 600 Boots Opticians stores. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Globally, pharmacy volume was impacted by a drop in doctor visits and hospital patient admissions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Additionally, gross margin was adversely impacted by sales mix, with a shift from higher margin discretionary categories to lower margin categories, and by
higher supply chain costs. The company took measures to keep stores open during <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> incurring incremental selling, general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A), including higher employee costs and
store expenses related to social distancing and incremental cleaning. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As a result of these impacts, operating and adjusted operating income included an
adverse impact of $700&nbsp;million to $750&nbsp;million, or $0.61 to $0.65 per share, excluding impairment charges. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Furthermore, considering the third
quarter operating loss in Boots UK and ongoing uncertainty due to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> the company reevaluated goodwill and intangibles in Boots UK, resulting in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT>
impairment charges of $2&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Accelerating Investments in Key Strategic Priorities </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the quarter the company prepared for future growth through aggressively accelerating investments in its four key strategic priorities. The impact of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> confirmed the company&#146;s existing strategy to take bold steps in creating neighborhood health destinations, driving cost transformation, digitalization and restructuring its retail offering. Below is a
summary of the most significant actions in the third quarter and since the end of the quarter: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Creating Neighborhood Health
Destinations </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As announced yesterday, WBA has taken an important step forward to accelerate its key strategic priority to create
neighborhood health destinations, through an integrated primary care and pharmacy delivery model that will drive better health outcomes, reduce healthcare costs and provide a differentiated patient experience. WBA and VillageMD announced that
Walgreens will be the first national pharmacy chain to offer full-service doctor offices <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-located</FONT> at its stores on a large scale, following a highly successful trial begun last year. This expanded
partnership will open 500 to 700 &#147;Village Medical at Walgreens&#148; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">physician-led</FONT> primary care clinics in more than 30 markets in the next five years, with the intent to build hundreds more thereafter.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The clinics will be staffed by more than 3,600 primary care providers, who will be recruited by VillageMD. The clinics will accept a wide
range of health insurance options and offer comprehensive primary care across a broad range of physician services. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the terms of the
new agreement, WBA will invest $1&nbsp;billion in equity and convertible debt in VillageMD over the next three years, including a $250&nbsp;million equity investment completed yesterday. Of WBA&#146;s investment, 80&nbsp;percent will be used by
VillageMD to fund the opening of the clinics and build the </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
partnership, including integration with Walgreens digital assets. It is anticipated, assuming full conversion of the debt, that WBA will hold an approximately 30&nbsp;percent ownership interest
in VillageMD at the completion of the investment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition, during the quarter, Walgreens and Boots UK both expanded their community
health roles by implementing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> testing sites. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Driving the Transformational Cost
Management Program </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the quarter, the company partly mitigated the impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> by
continuing to curtail costs while accelerating investments designed to drive long-term revenue growth. Cost containment across the company included temporary store closures, furloughing more than 16,000 UK employees at the peak of the crisis,
decreasing store hours and reducing rents at some locations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company is moving swiftly to address the impact of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> on the Boots business by accelerating the Boots Transformation Plan. Key elements of the proposed plan include a reorganization of the Boots store employee structure, the closure of 48 Boots Opticians
stores and an additional 20&nbsp;percent headcount reduction in the UK support office. Subject to labor consultation, these reorganization actions will impact more than 4,000 positions (7&nbsp;percent of the workforce). The Boots Transformation Plan
also includes increased investment and focus on the Boots omnichannel strategy and is designed to drive future growth in the company&#146;s UK market. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company increased its annual cost savings target from the Transformational Cost Management Program to in excess of $2.0&nbsp;billion by
fiscal 2022, from the previous target, which was annual cost savings in excess of $1.8&nbsp;billion by fiscal 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Accelerating
Digitalization </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As consumer behavior shifts rapidly, the company is increasing investments in omnichannel and in digital
infrastructure. The company is seeing encouraging response from customers to its digital marketing initiatives, with the ongoing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">roll-out</FONT> of mass personalization boosting Walgreens retail sales by 95 basis
points in the third quarter. Building on that approach, the company recently announced its strategic partnership with Microsoft and Adobe to launch a marketing technology and customer data platform to deliver personalized healthcare and shopping
experiences. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Transforming and Restructuring its Retail Offering </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Among many examples, Walgreens substantially built up its offering of personal protective equipment (PPE), added digital &#145;order
ahead&#146; drive-thru with an increased range of products available for drive-thru <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pick-up,</FONT> and put in place new delivery options. Walgreens total digitally initiated sales increased by 22.7&nbsp;percent in
the third quarter, compared with the same quarter a year ago. Boots UK also significantly boosted its Boots.com capabilities, investing in micro-fulfillment centers and hybrid stores and more than doubling capacity, which helped drive a
78&nbsp;percent increase in Boots.com sales in the quarter, compared with the same quarter a year ago, with continued strong performance in June. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Third Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal 2020 third
quarter net loss attributable to WBA was $1.7&nbsp;billion compared with net earnings of $1.0&nbsp;billion the same quarter a year ago. Net loss per share<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> was $1.95 compared with net earnings per
share (EPS) of $1.13 the same quarter a year ago. The results reflect $2&nbsp;billion in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges related to goodwill and intangible assets in Boots UK reflecting deteriorated business
conditions including the adverse impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> and resulting future uncertainty. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted net earnings attributable to WBA<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> decreased
45.9&nbsp;percent to $723&nbsp;million, down 45.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago. Adjusted earnings per share were $0.83 compared with $1.47 the same quarter a year ago, a decrease of
43.8&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and a decrease of 43.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Results included an estimated adverse impact from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic of $0.61 to $0.65 per share. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in the third quarter were $34.6&nbsp;billion, an increase of 0.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, and an
increase of 1.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, as the pandemic sharply curtailed footfall in retail pharmacies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company had an operating
loss of $1.6&nbsp;billion in the third quarter, compared to operating income of $1.2&nbsp;billion in the same quarter a year ago, primarily due to impairment charges in Boots UK of $2&nbsp;billion. Adjusted operating income was $919&nbsp;million, a
decrease of 46.5&nbsp;percent on a reported currency basis and a decrease of 46.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, including an estimated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of $700&nbsp;million to $750&nbsp;million.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $914&nbsp;million in the third quarter and free cash flow was $657&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2020 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the first nine months of fiscal 2020, net earnings attributable to WBA decreased 97.5&nbsp;percent to $83&nbsp;million compared with the same period a year
ago, while net earnings per share<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1 </SUP>decreased 97.3&nbsp;percent to $0.09 compared with the same period a year ago<I>. </I>The results reflect the impact of impairment charges in Boots UK. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted net earnings attributable to WBA<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> for the first nine months of fiscal 2020 decreased
22.6&nbsp;percent to $3.3&nbsp;billion, down 22.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same period a year ago. Adjusted earnings per share for the first nine months of fiscal 2020 were $3.72, a decrease of 18.5&nbsp;percent
on a reported basis and a decrease of 18.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same period a year ago. The results reflect an estimated adverse impact of $0.60 to $0.64 from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT>
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in the first nine months of fiscal 2020 were $105&nbsp;billion, an increase of 1.8&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago, and an increase of
2.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the first nine months of fiscal 2020 was $662&nbsp;million, a decrease of
83.9&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago. Adjusted operating income in the first nine months of the fiscal year was $4.1&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 24.1&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago on both a reported and constant currency
basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $3.4&nbsp;billion in the first nine months of fiscal 2020, an increase of $183&nbsp;million from the
same period last year, and free cash flow was $2.4&nbsp;billion, an increase of $467&nbsp;million, from the same period a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the third
quarter the company took significant proactive actions to improve financial flexibility, including securing $5.1&nbsp;billion of incremental facilities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company introduced fiscal 2020
adjusted EPS guidance of $4.65 to $4.75, including estimated adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impacts of $1.03 to $1.14 per share. This guidance assumes continued adverse impacts from
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> in the fourth quarter. In the UK, retail conditions are expected to remain very depressed, despite gradual easing of restrictions. More robust sales growth is expected in the Retail Pharmacy USA
division, although retail margins are expected to remain compressed in comparison to fiscal 2019. This guidance is based on sales trends the company saw in the month of June and does not factor in potential changes to those trends. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Dividend Increase and Share Repurchase Program Update </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&nbsp;8, 2020 the WBA board of directors declared a quarterly dividend of 46.75 cents per share, an increase of 2.2&nbsp;percent. The increased dividend
is payable September&nbsp;11, 2020 to stockholders of record as of August&nbsp;19, 2020, and raises the annual rate from $1.83 per share to $1.87 per share. This marks the 45th consecutive year that WBA and its predecessor company, Walgreen Co.,
have raised the dividend, and the 87th year a dividend has been paid. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company also announced that it was suspending activity under its share
repurchase program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Divisions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail
Pharmacy USA: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third quarter sales in Retail Pharmacy USA increased 3.2&nbsp;percent to $27.4&nbsp;billion, including the impact of previously
announced store closures. Sales in comparable stores increased 3.0&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Prescriptions filled in the third quarter decreased 1.3&nbsp;percent, compared with the same quarter a year earlier. In comparable stores, prescriptions
filled increased 0.4&nbsp;percent from a year earlier, a slower rate of growth than in the second quarter, as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">stay-at-home</FONT></FONT> orders led to a drop in doctor visits and hospital admissions. The prescription volume trend has shown steady improvement since the end of May. The number
of prescriptions filled was 287&nbsp;million, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents. Pharmacy sales increased 4.6&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, as higher brand inflation and a 15.9&nbsp;percent increase in specialty sales offset the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> prescription volume impact. Comparable pharmacy sales
increased 3.5&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The division&#146;s retail prescription market share on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> adjusted basis in
the third quarter was similar to the previous quarter and declined approximately 30 basis points over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to 20.9&nbsp;percent, as reported by IQVIA. This result included an adverse impact due
to the store closures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 0.7&nbsp;percent in the third quarter compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
period, including the impact of the store closures. Comparable retail sales were up 1.9&nbsp;percent in the quarter. Excluding tobacco and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> comparable retail sales increased 3.5&nbsp;percent.
Comparable retail sales were impacted by a change in shopping patterns in the quarter, with increased demand for vitamins and PPE leading to a 9&nbsp;percent increase in the health and wellness category. The personal care category increased
5&nbsp;percent, while declining demand for discretionary items led to a 9&nbsp;percent decrease in the beauty category. The general merchandise category was roughly flat, with an 8&nbsp;percent increase in sales of grocery and household products
offset by lower spending in discretionary areas, including a 34&nbsp;percent decrease in photo. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 9.6&nbsp;percent compared with the
same quarter a year ago and adjusted gross profit decreased 8.7&nbsp;percent. The company estimates that about 45&nbsp;percent of the year-over-year decline in gross profit was due to impacts related to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> such as the slow-down in pharmacy volume and the adverse gross profit mix, with most of the remaining impact due to ongoing reimbursement pressure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SG&amp;A increased by 4.4&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, mostly reflecting costs related to the
Transformational Cost Management Program, and adjusted SG&amp;A decreased by 0.4&nbsp;percent. Incremental COVID-19 related costs exceeded $100&nbsp;million in the third quarter, offset by Transformational Cost Management Program savings and
short-term actions to help mitigate the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the third quarter decreased
77.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $226&nbsp;million. Excluding costs related to the Transformational Cost Management Program, store damage and inventory loss incurred during looting in May, and
the acquisition of Rite Aid stores, adjusted operating income in the third quarter decreased 38.4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $792&nbsp;million. This included an estimated adverse <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of $325&nbsp;million to $350&nbsp;million or 25 to 27 percentage points. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">5 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail Pharmacy International: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail Pharmacy International had third quarter sales of $1.9&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 31.5&nbsp;percent from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 5.3&nbsp;percent. Sales decreased 26.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, mainly due to a 27.7&nbsp;percent decrease in Boots UK sales as foot
traffic in stores was severely disrupted by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> restrictions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable retail sales decreased
48.0&nbsp;percent. Boots UK lost share in its categories, in a sharply lower market, as lockdown measures impacted high streets and shopping centers and compelled consumers to consolidate shopping into grocers. This decrease was partially offset by
a 78&nbsp;percent increase in Boots.com sales, as the pandemic restrictions boosted online sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable pharmacy sales in Boots UK decreased
1.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower prescription volume and reduced demand for services during the pandemic, mitigated in part by timing on National Health Service (NHS) reimbursement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 39.6&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, including an adverse currency impact of 4.3&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross
profit decreased 36.2&nbsp;percent, on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower retail sales in Boots UK and lower retail gross margin, largely due to supply chain costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SG&amp;A in the quarter was $2.8&nbsp;billion, up from $993&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, due to impairment
charges. Adjusted SG&amp;A decreased by 15.3&nbsp;percent, or $147&nbsp;million, to $816&nbsp;million, including a favorable currency impact of 5.7&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency basis, adjusted SG&amp;A decreased 9.5&nbsp;percent, reflecting
short-term cost mitigation initiatives and savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating loss in the third quarter was
$2.2&nbsp;billion, compared to operating income of $119&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, primarily as a result of the $2&nbsp;billion in impairment charges. Adjusted operating income decreased
$308&nbsp;million, to an adjusted operating loss of $143&nbsp;million, including a favorable currency impact of $8&nbsp;million. On a constant currency basis, adjusted operating income decreased $316&nbsp;million. The estimated adverse <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact on adjusted operating income was $365&nbsp;million to $390&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Pharmaceutical Wholesale:
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmaceutical Wholesale had third quarter sales of $5.9&nbsp;billion, an increase of 0.6&nbsp;percent from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 4.8&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency basis, sales increased 5.3&nbsp;percent, led by the UK and Germany. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the third quarter was $350&nbsp;million, including a $243&nbsp;million gain from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen,
which reported a tax benefit from the permanent shutdown of its PharMEDium compounding business. This compared with operating income of $87&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a $16&nbsp;million
loss from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen, which reported an impairment of PharMEDium&#146;s assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income
increased 2.0&nbsp;percent to $271&nbsp;million, up 5.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting sales growth and a higher contribution from AmerisourceBergen, partially offset by lower gross margin. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA will hold a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-hour</FONT> conference call to discuss the third quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, July&nbsp;9, 2020. The conference call will be simulcast through the WBA investor relations website at:
<U>http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. A replay of the conference call will be archived on the website for 12 months after the call. </P>

</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is a global leader in retail and wholesale pharmacy, touching millions of lives every day through dispensing
and distributing medicines, its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. The company has more than 100 years of trusted health care heritage and innovation in community pharmacy and pharmaceutical wholesaling.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Including equity method investments, WBA has a presence in more than 25 countries, employs more than 440,000 people and has more than 18,750 stores. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA&#146;s purpose is to help people across the world lead healthier and happier lives. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a
healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. The company&#146;s businesses have been recognized for their Corporate Social Responsibility. Walgreens was named to FORTUNE* magazine&#146;s 2019 Companies that Change the World
list and Boots UK was recognized as Responsible Business of the Year 2019-2020 by Business in the Community. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA is included in FORTUNE&#146;s 2020 list
of the World&#146;s Most Admired Companies. This is the 27th consecutive year that WBA or its predecessor company, Walgreen Co., has been named to the list. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More company information is available at <U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under&nbsp;SEC&nbsp;rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial
measures calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in&nbsp;the United States&nbsp;(GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press
release, which are not calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s
financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press
release. The company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis (including the information under &#147;Company Outlook&#148; above) where it is unable to provide a
meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet
occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is
unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially
from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company also presents certain information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such
constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding
the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2020 comparable sales and prescriptions filled figures for the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions exclude the benefit
of this year&#146;s leap day. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions, comparable stores are defined as those that have been open for at least
12 consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for the first 12 months after
the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable stores for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable store sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales refer
to total sales, pharmacy sales and retail sales, respectively, in such stores. For the Retail Pharmacy USA division, comparable numbers of prescriptions refer to number of </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
prescriptions in such stores. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the
same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to the Retail Pharmacy International division, comparable store sales, comparable pharmacy sales and
comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant
currency calculations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>

equivalent prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators
presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered
superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other
companies. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Store damage and inventory losses as a result of looting in the U.S. during May 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Discrete <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-only</FONT> items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Represents the adjustment to the GAAP basis tax provision commensurate with
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and the adjusted tax rate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">true-up.</FONT> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Beginning in the quarter ended May&nbsp;31, 2019, management reviewed and refined its practice to reflect the
proportionate share of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in order
to provide investors with a comparable view of performance across periods. These adjustments include acquisition-related amortization and acquisition-related costs and were immaterial for the prior periods presented. Although the company may have
shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the company has direct control over their
operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from the reported net loss, the impact of potentially dilutive
securities on the per share amounts has been omitted from the quarterly calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted EPS for the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2020. The impact of these potentially dilutive securities has
been included in the calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted EPS for the nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes impact of potentially dilutive securities in the quarterly calculation of weighted-average common
shares, diluted for adjusted diluted net earnings per common share calculation purposes for the three and nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other
contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
